 China on Friday said that there has been no change in its stance on the entry into the Nuclear Suppliers Group (NSG) of countries that have not signed the Nuclear non-proliferation Treaty (NPT)
 china ke is bayaan se bharat ke 48 sadasyeey enesji main samooh kii agle saptaah hone vaali baithak main pravesh kii sambhaavna ko dhakka pahunchaa he
 China's Foreign Ministry spokesman Lu Kang told reporters, "on the issue of the Nuclear Suppliers Group (NSG), i can tell you that there has been no change in China's stance on the entry of new members into the NSG
" ' lu ne yah tippanee un khabaron ko lekar puche gaye sawaal kaa uttar dete hue kii ki roosi raashtrapati vladimir putin ne haal main astana main hue shanghai sahyog sanghathan (essio) sammelan ke itar china ke raashtrapati shi chinafing ke saath hui baithak main enesji main bharat ke pravesh kaa mudda uthaaya tha
 According to reports, the full meeting of the NSG is to be held in Bern, the capital of Switzerland, next week
 yah mudda bharat or china ke saath dwipaksheeya baithak main ek pramukh baadha ban gaya he
 After India's application for entry into this group governing the nuclear trade (NSG), Pakistan's evergreen ally Pakistan also applied with China's silent support
